Time Model Statistics

  • DB Time represents total time in user calls
  • DB CPU represents CPU time of foreground processes
  • Total CPU Time represents foreground and background processes
  • Statistics including the word "background" measure background process time, therefore do not contribute to the DB time statistic
  • Ordered by % of DB time in descending order, followed by Statistic Name

ATTR3 ABSENT ON NULL RETURNING CLOB) END AS OBJ FROM SYS.DBA_ADVISOR_OBJECTS WHERE TASK_ID = :B1 AND TYPE IN ('SQL', 'DATABASE OBJECT', 'DATABASE BLOCK', 'DATABASE FILE', 'TABLESPACE', 'DATABASE
